           <h2 class="fragment-heading">
            Dedicated to Your Comfort
           </h2>
           <hr class="short"/>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="row cols2 wrap-images">
          <div class="col span1">
           <p>
            At Dental Arts of New Hampshire,
            <a href="/about-our-team/the-doctors">
             Dr. Sameer Dogra and Dr. Ashley Pinette
            </a>
            are dedicated to providing a relaxing and stress-free atmosphere to all of our patients. We offer sedation dentistry, which not only keeps our patients comfortable, but enables us to perform multiple procedures in a single visit. Whether you need a routine cleaning or want to completely restore your smile with
            <a href="/procedures/dental-implants">
             dental implants
            </a>
            , our team has the tools and training to help you achieve your smile goals. We also have two convenient locations in Bedford and
            <strong>
             Salem, NH
            </strong>
            , so you can receive the treatment you need close to home.
           </p>

       <div class="quote-background" style="background-image: url('https://d1l9wtg77iuzz5.cloudfront.net/assets/5667/233425/original.jpg?1527891510'); background-position: 50%;opacity: 0.5;">

           <blockquote>
            <p>
             “
             <span>
              Dr. Sam is so personable. I enjoy his smiling face and his friendly mannerism. He installed a 3-tooth bridge and I am ecstatic. I was missing a tooth for such a long time, and the space drove me crazy. After evaluating the tooth and the situation, he suggested the bridge and I am thrilled with it.
             </span>
             ”
            </p>

           <p class="author">

      <section class="wrap full pure content-50-50-fragment is-default">
       <div class="box-inner">
        <div class="wrap fixed pure wide" data-lucid-group="Content-50-50 (3)">
         <div class="row cols1">
          <div class="col span1">
           <h2 class="fragment-heading">
            Innovative Periodontal Care
           </h2>
           <hr class="short"/>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="row cols2 wrap-images">
          <div class="col span1">
           <p>
            For patients with gum recession,
            <a href="/about-our-team">
             our team
            </a>
            offers the advanced Chao Pinhole® Surgical Technique. Invented by Dr. John Chao, this minimally invasive treatment can restore the health of your gums without scalpels, sutures, or grafts. Instead, we use a small pinhole to gently lower the gum tissue, covering exposed roots and creating a healthier smile. Compared to a traditional gum graft, the Pinhole Surgical Technique is a quick and easy way to combat the effects of gum recession. In addition, there is little to no downtime associated with this treatment. Most patients return to their normal activities the day of the procedure.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="col span1">
           <p>
            <img alt="Chao Pinhole® Surgical Technique" src="https://d1n5s2tett0dwr.cloudfront.net/A0hWm5pSFcg2DJ6hogXeSVX1Qg4=/700x/filters:no_upscale()/https://d3b3by4navws1f.cloudfront.net/chao-pinhole3.jpg"/>
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </section>

      <section class="wrap fixed pure wide section accurate-fragment is-default" data-lucid-group="AccuRate (1)">
       <div class="row cols1">
        <div class="col span1">
         <iframe data-full-height="254px" data-small-height="254px" id="accurate-iframe" scrolling="no" src="https://www.docshop.com/accurate/embed.php?style=2&amp;sbid=1631-71072082-4d7847e891349434c0142fd4212ba3cc1d6d2166&amp;s=http://www.dentalartsofnewhampshire.com/" style="width: 100%; height: 254px; overflow: hidden;">
         </iframe>
         <script>
          (function(){
   var el = document.getElementById('accurate-iframe');
   if (typeof el == 'undefined') { return; }
   var fullHeight = el.getAttribute('data-full-height');
   var smallHeight = el.getAttribute('data-small-height');
   if (fullHeight == smallHeight) { return; }
   var lastHeight = el.style.height;
   var resizer = function() {
     if (el.clientWidth < 960) {
       var newHeight = smallHeight;
     } else {
       var newHeight = fullHeight;
     }
     if (newHeight != lastHeight) {
       el.style.height = newHeight;
       lastHeight = newHeight;
     }
   };
   setInterval(resizer, 200);
 })();
         </script>
        </div>
       </div>
